	focus = {
		id = ENG_peaceful
		icon = GFX_goal_peace_with_our_neighbors
		x = -12
		y = 0
		cost = 40
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = limited_rearmament_focus focus = ENG_angry }
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
		
		available_if_capitulated = yes
		available = {
			has_war = no
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_war_support = -0.05
			every_other_country = {	
				limit = {
					not = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = communism
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
					num_of_factories > 25					
				}
				random_select_amount = 3
				add_opinion_modifier = { 
					target = ROOT 
					modifier = BUL_befriended_us
				} 
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = small_increase
				}
			}	
			every_owned_state = { 
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
					is_core_of = ROOT
					NOT = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
					NOT = { has_state_category = small_island }
				}
				random_select_amount = 7
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}	
			custom_effect_tooltip = modify_empire_TT
			add_to_variable = { british_stability = 0.01 tooltip = british_stability_tt }			
		}
	}

				tooltip = lon_good

			}
			has_war = no
			if = {
                limit = {
                    all_of_scopes = {
                        array = global.league_member
                        if = { 
                            limit = {
                                
                                NOT = { TAG = ENG }
                                has_opinion = {
                                    target = ENG
                                    value > 10
                                }
                            }
                            add_to_temp_variable = { vote_counter = 1 } # Assumed to be zero if unset
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
			set_temp_variable = { votes = vote_counter }
			divide_temp_variable = { votes = global.league_member^num }
			set_temp_variable = { votes_display = votes}
			multiply_temp_variable = { votes_display = 100 }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = ENG_vote_lon
				check_variable = { votes > 0.499 }
			}
				
			
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			unlock_decision_category_tooltip = ENG_league_of_nations
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = league_member
					is_major = yes
					not = { tag = CHI }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = jealous }
			}
		}

	focus = {

				limit = {

			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = { has_idea = ENG_stagnant_aviation_industry }
				}

					add_idea = ENG_stagnant_aviation_industry_reduced
					remove_idea = ENG_stagnant_aviation_industry
				}

					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}		
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			add_ideas = british_fighter_discount_I
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = { has_idea = ENG_stagnant_aviation_industry }
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = ENG_stagnant_aviation_industry_reduced
					remove_idea = ENG_stagnant_aviation_industry
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = ENG_focus_raf_1936
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = Line_break_keep_formating
				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_if_focus_raf_36
				effect_tooltip = {
					air_experience = 25
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 1
								include_locked = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
							NOT = { has_state_category = small_island }
						}
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 2
							instant_build = yes
						}
						set_state_flag = air_rearmament_focus_mil
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_branch_focused

			if = {

						is_ai = no
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
				OR = {
					threat > 0.03
					date > 1937.1.1
				}
			}
			else = {
				OR = {
					threat > 0.03
					date > 1936.6.1
				}
			}
		}
		continue_if_invalid = yes
		available_if_capitulated = yes

			if = {
				limit = {

			}
			else = {
				navy_experience = 25
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = ENG_naval_rearmament_focus_1dockyard }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = ENG_naval_rearmament_focus_1capitalshipyard }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = shipyard_capital_building
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			navy_experience = 25
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 133 }
				limit = {
					dockyard > 0
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_fully_controlled_by = ENG
					is_coastal = yes
					NOT = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
					NOT = { has_state_category = small_island }

				add_building_construction = {
					type = shipyard_capital_building
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = ENG_naval_rearmament_focus_1capitalshipyard
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					is_coastal = yes
					free_building_slots = {
						building = dockyard
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = ENG_naval_rearmament_focus_1dockyard
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = ENG_focus_navy_1936
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = Line_break_keep_formating
				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_if_focus_navy_only_36
				effect_tooltip = {
					navy_experience = 25
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							is_coastal = yes

							}
						}

							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}

					}
				}
			}
			if = {

				}

				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				add_core_of = ENG
			}
			NZL = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = ENG
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
			    target = NZL
			    transfer_troops = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = NZL
				}
				add_core_of = ENG
			}
			MAL = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = ENG
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
			    target = MAL
			    transfer_troops = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ENG_ahistorical_federation
				}
				clr_country_flag = ENG_ahistorical_federation
				set_country_flag = ENG_historical_path
			}
		}
	}

						limit = { is_ai = no }
						has_tech = tech_trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m2_1
						has_design_based_on = trm_medium_tank_chassis
					}
					else = {
						has_design_based_on = trm_medium_tank_chassis
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available_if_capitulated = yes
		
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Arms Against Tyranny"
				}
				add_equipment_subsidy = {
					cic = 12500
					equipment_type = trm_medium_tank_chassis
					seller_tags = { USA }
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						USA = {
							has_tech = tech_trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m4_2
							has_equipment = {
								trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m4_2 > 0
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m4_2 amount = 300 producer = USA }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						USA = {
							has_tech = tech_trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m4_1
									has_equipment = {
								trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m4_1 > 0
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m4_1 amount = 300 producer = USA }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						USA = {
							has_tech = tech_trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m3_1
							has_equipment = {
								trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m3_1 > 0
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m3_1 amount = 300 producer = USA }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						USA = {
							has_tech = tech_trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m2_1
							has_equipment = {
								trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m2_1 > 0
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = trm_medium_tank_chassis_usa_m2_1 amount = 300 producer = USA }
				}
			}
		}
	}
